; callan24.txt
;
; This is the "extension rom" pair that handles
; the boot from the Callan disk controller(s)
;
; Tom Trebisky  2-22-2022
;
; Interesting addresses

; 0xe0000 - never touches this (context reg / input switches)

; IO addresses on the multibus that I see in this ROM:
; 0x1ff900 - CFC
; 0x1ff8a0 - CWC
; 0x1ff880 - MSC (a multibus device I don't have)

; Based on the menus in this ROM, the unknown device is probably
; the "MSC-9205" winchester

; RAM
; 00000 - 3ffff is on board ram
; 40000 - xffff is multibus ram (as mapped by this ROM)

; examining the jumpers on the board, I see:
; the jumpers on our CWC seem to be 00A0
; the jumpers on our CFC seem to be 0100

; it looks to me like the base address for multibus IO
; is 0x1ff800 which would be consistent with the jumpers
; above.
; This mapping is set up by this extension ROM and differs
; from the base address set up by the bootroms and
; described in the manual.
; The manual though simply says 0x1f0000
; This is all about page map setup which places multibus IO
; for 0-0x7ff at 0x1ff800 to 0x1fffff
; This is a Callan mapping, and it differs
; from what the PM68K CPU manual describes.
; Note also that this Callan mapping requires that multibus IO
; cards be jumpered in the lower half of the address space.
; (i.e. with base addresses less than 0x800.

; the CPU board has 256K of ram
; it is from 0 to 0x3ffff
; addresses from 0x40000 on are apparently mapped to
; RAM on the multibus, which is eligible for DMA
; (unlike the ram on the CPU card).

; ---------------------------------------

; The first 4 bytes in this ROM must be "2e7c 0001"
; for this to be recognized as an extension ROM.
; when this is seen, the bootrom does a JSR to 0x400000
; (this ROM never returns)

; Here we move the stack up higher in onboard RAM
; we have 256K of onboard ram from 0 to 0x3ffff
; we move the stack to the 128K boundary

  400000:	2e7c 0001 fffe 	moveal #0x1fffe,%sp	; move stack
  400006:	6100 0002      	bsrw 0x40000a

  40000a:	201f           	movel %sp@+,%d0		; our return address
  40000c:	0480 0000 000a 	subil #0xa,%d0

; copy this ROM to ram at 0x20000.
; we move 16K bytes, which is just right for a pair of 8k roms
; once done, we jump into the copied image.
; Why do this?  Probably the ROM's work with wait states and
; the ram is faster with no wait states.
;
; Note that this means that all the disassembled addresses in
; the rest of the ROM are in that world.
; I redid the disassembly accordingly to avoid confusion.

  400012:	2040           	moveal %d0,%a0
  400014:	227c 0002 0000 	moveal #0x20000,%a1
  40001a:	203c 0000 0fff 	movel #0xfff,%d0
  400020:	22d8           	movel %a0@+,%a1@+
  400022:	51c8 fffc      	dbf %d0,0x400020
  400026:	4ef9 0002 002c 	jmp 0x2002c

; From now on, we are running in RAM
; note that this ROM will never return to
; the original bootrom

   2002c:	2e7c 0003 fffe 	moveal #0x3fffe,%sp	; top of onboard RAM

; zero this block (only 2 bytes long)
   20032:	203c 0002 3d26 	movel #0x23d26,%d0
   20038:	207c 0002 3d24 	moveal #0x23d24,%a0

   2003e:	20fc 0000 0000 	movel #0,%a0@+
   20044:	b1c0           	cmpal %d0,%a0
   20046:	65f6           	bcss 0x2003e

   20048:	4eb9 0002 0058 	jsr 0x20058		; call board_init
   2004e:	4eb9 0002 25ae 	jsr 0x225ae		; call MAIN
   20054:	6000 ffd6      	braw 0x2002c		; loop

; -----------------
; subroutine to do board initialization "board_init"

   20058:	4e56 fff4      	linkw %fp,#-12
   2005c:	48ee 3080 fff4 	moveml %d7/%a4-%a5,%fp@(-12)

   20062:	2a7c 00c0 0000 	moveal #0xc00000,%a5	; segment map
   20068:	4247           	clrw %d7
   2006a:	6014           	bras 0x20080
   2006c:	3007           	movew %d7,%d0
   2006e:	48c0           	extl %d0
   20070:	0680 0000 0f00 	addil #0xf00,%d0
   20076:	3a80           	movew %d0,%a5@
   20078:	dbfc 0000 8000 	addal #0x8000,%a5
   2007e:	5247           	addqw #1,%d7
   20080:	0c47 0040      	cmpiw #0x40,%d7
   20084:	6de6           	blts 0x2006c

   20086:	2a7c 00a0 0000 	moveal #0xa00000,%a5	; page map
   2008c:	4247           	clrw %d7
   2008e:	600c           	bras 0x2009c
   20090:	3007           	movew %d7,%d0
   20092:	48c0           	extl %d0
   20094:	3a80           	movew %d0,%a5@
   20096:	dafc 0800      	addaw #0x800,%a5
   2009a:	5247           	addqw #1,%d7
   2009c:	0c47 0080      	cmpiw #0x80,%d7
   200a0:	6dee           	blts 0x20090

   200a2:	4247           	clrw %d7
   200a4:	6012           	bras 0x200b8
   200a6:	3007           	movew %d7,%d0
   200a8:	48c0           	extl %d0
   200aa:	0080 0000 2000 	oril #0x2000,%d0
   200b0:	3a80           	movew %d0,%a5@
   200b2:	dafc 0800      	addaw #0x800,%a5
   200b6:	5247           	addqw #1,%d7
   200b8:	0c47 0100      	cmpiw #0x100,%d7
   200bc:	6de8           	blts 0x200a6

   200be:	2a7c 00bf f800 	moveal #0xbff800,%a5
   200c4:	4247           	clrw %d7
   200c6:	6012           	bras 0x200da
   200c8:	3007           	movew %d7,%d0
   200ca:	48c0           	extl %d0
   200cc:	0080 0000 3000 	oril #0x3000,%d0
   200d2:	3a80           	movew %d0,%a5@
   200d4:	dafc 0800      	addaw #0x800,%a5
   200d8:	5247           	addqw #1,%d7
   200da:	0c47 0001      	cmpiw #1,%d7
   200de:	6de8           	blts 0x200c8

   200e0:	287c 0004 0000 	moveal #0x40000,%a4
   200e6:	6006           	bras 0x200ee
   200e8:	28fc 0000 0001 	movel #1,%a4@+
   200ee:	b9fc 0005 0000 	cmpal #0x50000,%a4
   200f4:	65f2           	bcss 0x200e8

   200f6:	4cee 3080 fff4 	moveml %fp@(-12),%d7/%a4-%a5
   200fc:	4e5e           	unlk %fp
   200fe:	4e75           	rts

; ========================================
; subroutine - just rearranges arguments and calls memcpy

   20100:	4e56 fff4      	linkw %fp,#-12
   20104:	4a2f ff7c      	tstb %sp@(-132)			; why??
   20108:	48ee 3080 fff4 	moveml %d7/%a4-%a5,%fp@(-12)	; save 3 regs

   2010e:	2a6e 0008      	moveal %fp@(8),%a5		; arg1
   20112:	286e 000c      	moveal %fp@(12),%a4		; arg2
   20116:	2e2e 0010      	movel %fp@(16),%d7		; arg3

   2011a:	2f07           	movel %d7,%sp@-		; push arg3
   2011c:	4855           	pea %a5@		; push arg1
   2011e:	4854           	pea %a4@		; push arg2
   20120:	4eb9 0002 2ad8 	jsr 0x22ad8
   20126:	defc 000c      	addaw #0xc,%sp

   2012a:	4cee 3080 fff4 	moveml %fp@(-12),%d7/%a4-%a5
   20130:	4e5e           	unlk %fp
   20132:	4e75           	rts

; =========================
; subroutine - big_delay ( arg )

   20134:	4e56 fff4      	linkw %fp,#-12
   20138:	48ee 00e0 fff4 	moveml %d5-%d7,%fp@(-12)

   2013e:	2e2e 0008      	movel %fp@(8),%d7	; d7 = arg
   20142:	7c00           	moveq #0,%d6		; d6 = 0
   20144:	6010           	bras 0x20156

; loop
   20146:	7a00           	moveq #0,%d5		; d5 = 0
   20148:	6002           	bras 0x2014c

   2014a:	5285           	addql #1,%d5		; delay spin
   2014c:	0c85 0003 a980 	cmpil #0x3a980,%d5	; 240,000
   20152:	6df6           	blts 0x2014a

   20154:	5286           	addql #1,%d6
   20156:	bc87           	cmpl %d7,%d6
   20158:	6dec           	blts 0x20146

   2015a:	4cee 00e0 fff4 	moveml %fp@(-12),%d5-%d7
   20160:	4e5e           	unlk %fp
   20162:	4e75           	rts

; =========================
; subroutine -- count_nz ( buf )

   20164:	4e56 fff8      	linkw %fp,#-8
   20168:	2f0d           	movel %a5,%sp@-
   2016a:	2f07           	movel %d7,%sp@-

   2016c:	2a6e 0008      	moveal %fp@(8),%a5	; a5 = arg
   20170:	7e00           	moveq #0,%d7		; d7 = 0
   20172:	6002           	bras 0x20176

; loop, count non-zero bytes
   20174:	5287           	addql #1,%d7
   20176:	4a1d           	tstb %a5@+
   20178:	66fa           	bnes 0x20174

   2017a:	2007           	movel %d7,%d0		; return count

   2017c:	2e1f           	movel %sp@+,%d7
   2017e:	2a5f           	moveal %sp@+,%a5
   20180:	4e5e           	unlk %fp
   20182:	4e75           	rts

; =========================
; subroutine strcmp ( a, b )
; compare two null terminated strings
; string "a" governs the termination

   20184:	4e56 fff4      	linkw %fp,#-12
   20188:	48ee 3080 fff4 	moveml %d7/%a4-%a5,%fp@(-12)

   2018e:	2a6e 0008      	moveal %fp@(8),%a5	; a5 = arg1
   20192:	286e 000c      	moveal %fp@(12),%a4	; a4 = arg2

; loop
   20196:	1e1d           	moveb %a5@+,%d7
   20198:	be1c           	cmpb %a4@+,%d7
   2019a:	6608           	bnes 0x201a4
   2019c:	4a07           	tstb %d7
   2019e:	66f6           	bnes 0x20196

   201a0:	7001           	moveq #1,%d0		; return 1
   201a2:	6002           	bras 0x201a6

   201a4:	7000           	moveq #0,%d0		; return 0

   201a6:	4cee 3080 fff4 	moveml %fp@(-12),%d7/%a4-%a5
   201ac:	4e5e           	unlk %fp
   201ae:	4e75           	rts

; =====================
; subroutine, move ( src, dest )
; copys null terminated string

   201b0:	4e56 fffc      	linkw %fp,#-4
   201b4:	4a2f ff7c      	tstb %sp@(-132)

   201b8:	2f2e 0008      	movel %fp@(8),%sp@-
   201bc:	4eb9 0002 0164 	jsr 0x20164		; n = count_nz ( arg1 )
   201c2:	588f           	addql #4,%sp

   201c4:	5280           	addql #1,%d0		; n + 1
   201c6:	2d40 fffc      	movel %d0,%fp@(-4)	; save d0 (silly)

   201ca:	2f00           	movel %d0,%sp@-		; count
   201cc:	2f2e 000c      	movel %fp@(12),%sp@-	; arg2 (dest)
   201d0:	2f2e 0008      	movel %fp@(8),%sp@-	; arg1 (src)
   201d4:	4eb9 0002 01e2 	jsr 0x201e2
   201da:	defc 000c      	addaw #0xc,%sp

   201de:	4e5e           	unlk %fp
   201e0:	4e75           	rts

; =====================
; subroutine (called from above)
;
; strncpy ( src, dest, N )

   201e2:	4e56 fff4      	linkw %fp,#-12
   201e6:	48ee 3080 fff4 	moveml %d7/%a4-%a5,%fp@(-12)

   201ec:	2a6e 0008      	moveal %fp@(8),%a5	; a5 = arg1 (src)
   201f0:	286e 000c      	moveal %fp@(12),%a4	; a4 = arg2 (dest)
   201f4:	2e2e 0010      	movel %fp@(16),%d7	; d7 = arg3 (count)
   201f8:	6002           	bras 0x201fc
   201fa:	18dd           	moveb %a5@+,%a4@+	; *a4++ = *a5++
   201fc:	2007           	movel %d7,%d0		; d0 = d7
   201fe:	5387           	subql #1,%d7
   20200:	4a80           	tstl %d0
   20202:	66f6           	bnes 0x201fa

   20204:	4cee 3080 fff4 	moveml %fp@(-12),%d7/%a4-%a5
   2020a:	4e5e           	unlk %fp
   2020c:	4e75           	rts

   2020e:	4e56 fff4      	linkw %fp,#-12
   20212:	48ee 20c0 fff4 	moveml %d6-%d7/%a5,%fp@(-12)
   20218:	2a6e 0008      	moveal %fp@(8),%a5
   2021c:	1e2e 000f      	moveb %fp@(15),%d7
   20220:	2c2e 0010      	movel %fp@(16),%d6
   20224:	6002           	bras 0x20228
   20226:	1ac7           	moveb %d7,%a5@+
   20228:	2006           	movel %d6,%d0
   2022a:	5386           	subql #1,%d6
   2022c:	4a80           	tstl %d0
   2022e:	66f6           	bnes 0x20226
   20230:	4cee 20c0 fff4 	moveml %fp@(-12),%d6-%d7/%a5
   20236:	4e5e           	unlk %fp
   20238:	4e75           	rts
   2023a:	4e56 ffe8      	linkw %fp,#-24
   2023e:	4a2f ff7c      	tstb %sp@(-132)

   20248:	2a6e 0008      	moveal %fp@(8),%a5
   2024c:	2e2e 000c      	movel %fp@(12),%d7

   20252:	0686 0000 000f 	addil #0xf,%d6
   20258:	e886           	asrl #4,%d6
   2025a:	2f3c 0000 000a 	movel #0xa,%sp@-
   20260:	4eb9 0002 1734 	jsr 0x21734		; putc
   20266:	588f           	addql #4,%sp
   20268:	7a00           	moveq #0,%d5
   2026a:	6000 00ac      	braw 0x20318

   20a60:	4e5e           	unlk %fp

; How does linkw work?
; First it pushes the specified register (fp in general)
; onto the stack.
; Then that register is loaded with the updated stack pointer.
; Then the displacement (generally negative) is added to
; the stack pointer
;
; This allocates a block of stuff (with the stack pointing to it)
; 
; linkw is paired with "unlk"
; note that unlk has no need to know the displacement used by linkw
; it just loads the stack pointer from the %fp register
; then it pops the stack into the %fp register
;
; In the following routine, the displacement is 24, which is
; 6 words of 4 bytes each, just enough space for the stuff
; dumped by the moveml that follows

; subroutine "hd_wait"
   20a64:	4e56 ffe8      	linkw %fp,#-24
   20a68:	4a2f ff7c      	tstb %sp@(-132)
   20a6c:	48ee 38e0 ffe8 	moveml %d5-%d7/%a3-%a5,%fp@(-24)

   20a72:	2a7c 001f f8a0 	moveal #0x1ff8a0,%a5		; multibus - CWC

; poll to see if ready
   20a78:	7e00           	moveq #0,%d7		; d7 = 0
   20a7a:	2c3c 0007 a120 	movel #0x7a120,%d6	; d6 = 500,000
   20a80:	600a           	bras 0x20a8c

   20a82:	082d 0007 0001 	btst #7,%a5@(1)		; test busy
   20a88:	6706           	beqs 0x20a90
   20a8a:	5287           	addql #1,%d7		; d7++
   20a8c:	be86           	cmpl %d6,%d7
   20a8e:	6df2           	blts 0x20a82		; try again

; here when busy is found clear
   20a90:	be86           	cmpl %d6,%d7		; did we time out
   20a92:	6610           	bnes 0x20aa4		; nope

; here if we timed out waiting to not be busy
   20a94:	2f07           	movel %d7,%sp@-
   20a96:	2f3c 0002 2fed 	movel #0x22fed,%sp@-
   20a9c:	4eb9 0002 193e 	jsr 0x2193e		; printf
   20aa2:	508f           	addql #8,%sp

; the following tests our argument (some kind of flag)
   20aa4:	4aae 0008      	tstl %fp@(8)		; check flag
   20aa8:	673e           	beqs 0x20ae8		; return if 0

   20aaa:	287c 0004 0800 	moveal #0x40800,%a4	; in ROM
   20ab0:	267c 0004 0900 	moveal #0x40900,%a3	; in ROM

   20ab6:	1b79 0002 2fb0 	moveb 0x22fb0,%a5@(6)
   20abc:	0006
   20abe:	1a2b 0001      	moveb %a3@(1),%d5
   20ac2:	0285 0000 00f0 	andil #0xf0,%d5
   20ac8:	0c05 0080      	cmpib #0xff80,%d5
   20acc:	671a           	beqs 0x20ae8		; return

   20ace:	0c05 00a0      	cmpib #0xffa0,%d5
   20ad2:	6714           	beqs 0x20ae8		; return

   20ad4:	0c05 00ff      	cmpib #-1,%d5
   20ad8:	670e           	beqs 0x20ae8		; return

   20ada:	4a05           	tstb %d5
   20adc:	670a           	beqs 0x20ae8		; return

   20ade:	2f0b           	movel %a3,%sp@-
   20ae0:	4eb9 0002 0a14 	jsr 0x20a14
   20ae6:	588f           	addql #4,%sp

; So, we have an address in a4, it is a multibus address
; from the CPU perspective.

; ========================================================
; subroutine - send a character. "putc"
; it seems crazy, but this seems to initialize the uart and timer
; for each and every character.
; actually it doesn't.  There is a lock/flag in the init routine

   21734:	4e56 fff4	linkw %fp,#-12
   21738:	4a2f ff7c      	tstb %sp@(-132)
   2173c:	48ee 20c0 fff4 	moveml %d6-%d7/%a5,%fp@(-12)
   21742:	2e2e 0008      	movel %fp@(8),%d7

   21746:	4eb9 0002 17de 	jsr 0x217de		; uart init

   2174c:	2a7c 0060 0000 	moveal #0x600000,%a5	; uart base
   21752:	0c87 0000 000a 	cmpil #0xa,%d7
   21758:	660e           	bnes 0x21768

   2175a:	2f3c 0000 000d 	movel #0xd,%sp@-	; push a CR
   21760:	4eb9 0002 1734 	jsr 0x21734		; recursion
   21766:	588f           	addql #4,%sp

; polling with timeout of 200,000
; until the uart is ready to send another character
   21768:	2c3c 0003 0d40 	movel #0x30d40,%d6	; 200000
   2176e:	082d 0002 0002 	btst #2,%a5@(2)

   21780:	0280 0000 007f 	andil #0x7f,%d0
   21786:	1a80           	moveb %d0,%a5@		; send character

   2178e:	4e5e           	unlk %fp
   21790:	4e75           	rts

; subroutine to read character "getc"

; subroutine -- the last in this ROM !
; call this mul32

   22df4:	48e7 3000      	moveml %d2-%d3,%sp@-
   22df8:	242f 000c      	movel %sp@(12),%d2	; arg1
   22dfc:	262f 0010      	movel %sp@(16),%d3	; arg2

; mulu is 16x16 = 32
; swap exchanges 16 bit halves
; let d2 = A -- B
; let d3 = C -- D

   22e00:	3002           	movew %d2,%d0		; d0 = B
   22e02:	c0c3           	muluw %d3,%d0		; d0 = B * D

   22e04:	3202           	movew %d2,%d1		; d1 = B
   22e06:	4842           	swap %d2		; B -- A
   22e08:	c4c3           	muluw %d3,%d2		; d2 = A * D

   22e0a:	4843           	swap %d3		; D -- C
   22e0c:	c2c3           	muluw %d3,%d1		; d1 = B * C

   22e0e:	d282           	addl %d2,%d1		; d1 = B*C + A*D
   22e10:	4841           	swap %d1
   22e12:	4241           	clrw %d1		; <<16
   22e14:	d081           	addl %d1,%d0

   22e16:	4cdf 000c      	moveml %sp@+,%d2-%d3
   22e1a:	4e75           	rts
